          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer836214783" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12769279488142413204"><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/4973548_zps836cc80b.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382545801ra/5977300.gif' alt='crying photo 4973548_zps836cc80b.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"This is at once the end and the beginning. This is the story of my love of two men. One is my father. The other is a man who fell from the sky." </i>
</b><br/> <br/>Benji is a twenty-something year old gay man who lives in a small town. His father owned a gas station and he now runs it since his father passed away. He has this recurring dream where he is drowning. He is drowning and surrounded by blue. He is drowning, surrounded by blue, and his father is there. It’s the site where his father had his acci</span>
  <span id="freeText12769279488142413204" style="display:none"><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/4973548_zps836cc80b.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382545801ra/5977300.gif" alt="crying photo 4973548_zps836cc80b.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>"This is at once the end and the beginning. This is the story of my love of two men. One is my father. The other is a man who fell from the sky." </i>
</b><br> <br>Benji is a twenty-something year old gay man who lives in a small town. His father owned a gas station and he now runs it since his father passed away. He has this recurring dream where he is drowning. He is drowning and surrounded by blue. He is drowning, surrounded by blue, and his father is there. It’s the site where his father had his accident. He is constantly haunted by the river at mile marker 77. <br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/tumblr_n10bcpDdKb1trmvswo1_500_zps7f5aa7cf.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393213167ra/8677452.gif" alt="drown photo tumblr_n10bcpDdKb1trmvswo1_500_zps7f5aa7cf.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Finally after one of these episodes Benji's grief is overwhelming him and something happens. A big light falls from the sky and down comes Calliel. He is very attractive and tells Benji he is the guardian angel of Roseland. He has fallen to the Earth because Benji called out for him.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/0de846c0-80c9-4ed7-af31-20b4437674ad_zpsfc98f315.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393213939i/8677667.jpg" alt=" photo 0de846c0-80c9-4ed7-af31-20b4437674ad_zpsfc98f315.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>They nickname him Cal Blue and they tell everyone he is from California to explain his oddball behavior. Cal and Benji are attracted to each other but Benji doesn't feel he can have a relationship with an angel, plus is Cal even gay? Can angels be gay?<br><br>Everyone in Roseland loves Cal and accepts him no questions asked. This is a small town but they band together for each other. They love Benji and come to love Cal as well. Even with his quirks (such as a love for clover marshmallow in lucky charms )<br> <br>Eventually it all goes down though and they get together! Woot Woot!<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/tumblr_mu3qs7crZr1syjenho1_500_zpsc0c8d510.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393213585ra/8677503.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mu3qs7crZr1syjenho1_500_zpsc0c8d510.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><b>
  <i>”I shouldn’t because it’s not what I was made for. It’s not why I came to be. But yes, Benji. God help me yes. I don’t want anything more than you. I want nothing less than you.”</i>
</b><br><br>But then the mystery still remains on what happened to Benji’s dad, Big Eddie. Benji misses his dad. Big Eddie sounds like he was an awesome person too. He supported Benji in every way.<br><br><b>
  <i>"If it takes all I have and if it means I will never be found, then so be it! For my family, for my son, into this river I drown! "</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY/tumblr_mcztp5ylLb1rum5tfo4_500_zps7f69c3ea.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391187668ra/8343960.gif" alt="crying photo tumblr_mcztp5ylLb1rum5tfo4_500_zps7f69c3ea.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Something odd is going on in Roseland though. The Sheriff is acting weird and seems out to get Benji. Calliel will keep him safe though. Cal is Benji's guardian. He is the protector. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Father, forgive me for what I must do. I pray for you to have faith in me as I do in you. The thread is bright. Benjamin Edward Green is mine, and I will do what I must do protect him.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393215788ra/8677894.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's a short time but yes they fall in love with each other. And its so beautiful.<br><br><b>
  <i>"He turns his head and places a gentle kiss to the place where my heart beats. The action is one of such singular beauty that I’m annihilated. If this is what he can give me, then I will take it all. And I will give back just the same."</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY/tumblr_mpf78uqqyO1qii8hro1_500_zps9ab9d1db.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380410910ra/806366.gif" alt="love photo tumblr_mpf78uqqyO1qii8hro1_500_zps9ab9d1db.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Benji wants to know what happened with his father's accident but for some reason Calliel has that memory blocked since his fall. Benji is determined but does he really want to find out the truth?<br><br><b>
  <i>"Sometimes the past is better left alone."</i>
</b><br><br>And once he finally finds out the truth, what will he do with it? What sacrifices will have to be made?<br><br><b>
  <i>"What a person does for the greater good defines who they are. A man should never be measured by how full his life is, but what he is willing to give up in order to protect those he loves."</i>
</b><br><br>And the end....Oh the ending..<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/tumblr_mn7monIUP61qlk4meo2_250_zps20e43110.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385072169ra/7060847.gif" alt="CRIED photo tumblr_mn7monIUP61qlk4meo2_250_zps20e43110.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY/tumblr_m3pg9du5d11qldudx_zps7bb6cf65.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394404ra/759391.gif" alt="crying photo tumblr_m3pg9du5d11qldudx_zps7bb6cf65.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> Let me end by saying this book is weird. Weird but good. The writing is somewhat strange because you are only being given pieces of everything in the beginning and it somewhat comes together toward the end. Not everyone will love it and it may not be for you but I encourage you to try and read it. I think you will love it as much as I did. And I know it seems like I put a ton of quotes and my review probably makes absolutely no sense but all I can say is just read the book. It's just an overall beautiful story.<br><br> <br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3651780287255014272"><b> <i>4-4.5 IMPOSSIBLE IMPROBABLE ABYYSS OF ANGST DRIVIN STARS!</i><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469279145ra/19800320.gif' width='400' height='300' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>-<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469279781i/19800396._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='450' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>into the river I drown</b><br/><br/>I LOVE philosophical reads...they just work for me, and add PNR. and I'm in HEAVEN. <br/><br/>The BIG treasures I found within this book: <br/><br/>The romance was ADORBS. <br/>The PNR touch is awesome. Angels I love. <br/>The action was thrilling. <br/>The Christian touches was fantastic.<br/>I have the e-book and audiobook with <b>Matt Baca, I found he is a gifted narrator</b> , I love how he drew me in. There were changing in the characters by voice, and GAWD</span>
  <span id="freeText3651780287255014272" style="display:none"><b> <i>4-4.5 IMPOSSIBLE IMPROBABLE ABYYSS OF ANGST DRIVIN STARS!</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469279145ra/19800320.gif" width="400" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg">-<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469279781i/19800396._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="450" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>into the river I drown</b><br><br>I LOVE philosophical reads...they just work for me, and add PNR. and I'm in HEAVEN. <br><br>The BIG treasures I found within this book: <br><br>The romance was ADORBS. <br>The PNR touch is awesome. Angels I love. <br>The action was thrilling. <br>The Christian touches was fantastic.<br>I have the e-book and audiobook with <b>Matt Baca, I found he is a gifted narrator</b> , I love how he drew me in. There were changing in the characters by voice, and GAWD Cal's voice * be still my heart* loved. <br><br>The narrators voice of song....well, he can sing, ever so sweetly and ever so softly. I heard him by way of Benji's dad and when Benji sang with him, it was grand. I found the voice(s) to be calm and soothing, and gosh, the song used just fit.<br><br>2/15/2020, Thid book was a little depressing, but , I still love it. It was worth the heart.<br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/605905953?book_show_action=true">May 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bitchie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bitchie" href="/user/show/7602015-bitchie">Bitchie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7602015-bitchie?shelf=fucking-loved-it">fucking-loved-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7602015-bitchie?shelf=m-m-romance">m-m-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7602015-bitchie?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7602015-bitchie?shelf=angels-and-demons">angels-and-demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7602015-bitchie?shelf=angsty">angsty</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer605905953" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5928232394292450926"><a href='http://imgur.com/pI6GNT5' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391131674ra/8334896.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Long and angsty and sad, I did the ugly cry near the end. In fact, I went and hid in the bathroom to read a big chunk of the end of it, and then came back and read on my tablet with the lights out, so hubby couldn't see my red eyes and puffy nose.<br/><br/>While this IS a love story with a HEA, at it's heart, this is more of a story about the love between a father and son, and the grief everyone feels when a truly good man dies.<br/><br/>My only real complaint was who the "Boss" ended up being, it seemed out of</span>
  <span id="freeText5928232394292450926" style="display:none"><a href="http://imgur.com/pI6GNT5" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391131674ra/8334896.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Long and angsty and sad, I did the ugly cry near the end. In fact, I went and hid in the bathroom to read a big chunk of the end of it, and then came back and read on my tablet with the lights out, so hubby couldn't see my red eyes and puffy nose.<br><br>While this IS a love story with a HEA, at it's heart, this is more of a story about the love between a father and son, and the grief everyone feels when a truly good man dies.<br><br>My only real complaint was who the "Boss" ended up being, it seemed out of left field, but the rest of the book was so good, I'm not going to quibble.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5928232394292450926" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_587570912" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/587570912" />
    <a title="Sandra " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5034547-sandra"><img alt="Sandra " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1413920321p2/5034547.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/587570912?book_show_action=true">Apr 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sandra " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sandra " href="/user/show/5034547-sandra">Sandra </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5034547-sandra?shelf=nailbiters">nailbiters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5034547-sandra?shelf=must-read">must-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5034547-sandra?shelf=supernatural">supernatural</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5034547-sandra?shelf=2013-book-challenge">2013-book-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5034547-sandra?shelf=m-m-yeah-baby">m-m-yeah-baby</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5034547-sandra?shelf=cry-me-a-river">cry-me-a-river</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5034547-sandra?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5034547-sandra?shelf=angels">angels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5034547-sandra?shelf=made-of-win">made-of-win</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5034547-sandra?shelf=angst-and-drama">angst-and-drama</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer587570912" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18364865070208956443">All the awards!!! All the awards for this book!! Go, buy it, read it, rejoice. <br/><br/>I still can't write a coherent review for this book. I wish I could give it more stars.<br/><br/>This book. This book!! It gutted me, gleefully ripped out and stomped on my heart, and then with a 'there, there' pat on the head, gave me a wee bit of happiness at the end. Wee meaning teeny-tiny, barely enough to stop me from drowning in my own tears.<br/><br/>That's all I have to say about that. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer712446259" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16216477410658500353"><br/><br/>Oh, oh, what a story.<br/><br/>Evocative prose written with a quiet, lilting rhythm, so subtle. Deeply graphic imagery, wildly imaginitve plot. Beautiful, richly-drawn characters. A heartbreaking beginning. A love-affirming ending. A gripping ride the whole way.<br/><br/>Read it!</span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('byThCrk5VgUp+CsW6Za0yEdG9usn9fCmcB3ViPij/dVrgjaHwTrhDVRiTXt97nSq/gmfsgp/bftLrR1yNxDuXQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('TjynNz65MsC2VYHYqJIsyoEhU9N5d1SRmldCkJK741dKmnC6RrqFyMvP57U86uyoOG46ilT9ycyh54pqXQjw3w==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer890555742267811676">TJ KLUNE is a Lambda Literary Award-winning author (Into This River I Drown) and an ex-claims examiner for an insurance company. His novels include The House in the Cerulean Sea and The Extraordinaries. Being queer himself, TJ believes it's important—now more than ever—to have accurate, positive, queer representation in stories.</span>
